#Amyzonis' AN overhaul of formables

country_decisions = {

#### Post-Discovery Formables
# Lusitania
AN_lusitania_nation = {
	major = yes
	potential = {
		NOT = { has_country_flag = formed_lusitania_flag }
		LSA = { exists = no }
		IBE = { exists = no }
		NOT = {
			OR = {
				government = native
				government = tribal
				tag = SPA
				tag = SPI
				tag = VSC
				tag = ADL
				tag = ADU
			}
			religion_group = muslim #Andalusia for Muslims
		}
		OR = {
			primary_culture = portugese
			primary_culture = galician
			primary_culture = asturian
			primary_culture = leonese
			primary_culture = extremaduran
		}
	}
	provinces_to_highlight = {
		province_group = lusitania_group
	}
	allow = {
		is_at_war = no
		has_institution = bureaucracy
		has_institution = printing_press
		adm_tech = 19 #Res Publica
		num_of_provinces_owned_or_owned_by_non_sovereign_subjects_with = {
			province_group = lusitania_group
			value = 60 #42 + (0.5 * 34) = 59 -> 60
		}
		227 = { country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT }
		231 = { country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT }
		208 = { country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT }
		206 = { country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT }
	}
	effect = {
		#Integrate PUs, Domains, Fiefs
		every_subject_country = {
			limit = { capital_scope = { province_group = lusitania_group } OR = { is_subject_of_type = personal_union is_subject_of_type = dominion is_subject_of_type = fief } }
			custom_tooltip = IR_formable_integration
			hidden_effect = {
				overlord = {
					inherit = PREV
				}
			}
		}

		#Change Tag
		change_tag = LSA

		#Set Govt Rank
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { government_rank = 4 } }
			set_government_rank = 4
		}

		#Rewards
		add_prestige = 25
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = centralization_modifier
			duration = 7300
		}

		#Change Ideas
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_custom_ideas = no
				NOT = { has_idea_group = LSA_ideas }
			}
			country_event = { id = ideagroups.1 } #Swap Ideas
		}

		#Disable decision
		set_country_flag = formed_lusitania_flag
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1
	}
	ai_importance = 400 #
}

# Spain
AN_spain_nation = {
	major = yes
	potential = {
		NOT = { has_country_flag = formed_spain_flag }
		SPA = { exists = no }
		IBE = { exists = no }
		NOT = {
			OR = {
				government = native
				government = tribal
				tag = LSA
				tag = SPI
				tag = VSC
				tag = ADL
				tag = ADU
			}
			religion_group = muslim #Andalusia for Muslims
		}
		OR = {
			primary_culture = castillian	
			primary_culture = asturian
			primary_culture = leonese
			primary_culture = extremaduran
			primary_culture = aragonese
			primary_culture = toledan
			primary_culture = murcian
		}
	}
	provinces_to_highlight = {
		province_group = spain_group
	}
	allow = {
		is_at_war = no
		has_institution = bureaucracy
		has_institution = printing_press
		adm_tech = 19 #Res Publica
		num_of_provinces_owned_or_owned_by_non_sovereign_subjects_with = {
			province_group = spain_group
			value = 120 #96 + 20 (0.5 * 34) = 59 -> 60
		}
		217 = { country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT }
		219 = { country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT }
		1746 = { country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT }
		214 = { country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT }
	}
	effect = {
		#Integrate PUs, Domains, Fiefs
		every_subject_country = { 
			limit = { capital_scope = { province_group = spain_group } OR = { is_subject_of_type = personal_union is_subject_of_type = dominion is_subject_of_type = fief } }
			custom_tooltip = IR_formable_integration
			hidden_effect = {
				overlord = {
					inherit = PREV
				}
			}
		}
		
		#Change Tag
		change_tag = SPA	
		
		#Set Govt Rank	
		if = { 
			limit = { NOT = { government_rank = 4 } }
			set_government_rank = 4
		}
		
		#Rewards
		add_prestige = 25
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = centralization_modifier
			duration = 7300
		}
		
		#Change Ideas
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_custom_ideas = no
				NOT = { has_idea_group = SPA_ideas }
			}
			country_event = { id = ideagroups.1 } #Swap Ideas
		}
		
		#Disable decision
		set_country_flag = formed_spain_flag
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1
	}
	ai_importance = 400 #
}

# Al-Andalus
AN_al_andalus_nation = { 
	major = yes
	potential = {
		NOT = { has_country_flag = formed_al_andalus_flag }
		ADL = { exists = no }
		ADU = { exists = no }
		IBE = { exists = no }
		NOT = { 
			OR = { 
				government = native 
				government = tribal
				tag = LSA
				tag = SPA
				tag = SPI
				tag = VSC
				tag = ADL
			}
		}
		religion_group = muslim #Al-Andalus for Muslims
		OR = {
			primary_culture = andalusi_culture
			AND = {
				culture_group = turko_semitic #Arabic
				any_owned_province = { region = iberia_region }
			}
			AND = {
				culture_group = berber
				any_owned_province = { region = iberia_region }
			}
		}
	}
	provinces_to_highlight = {
		province_group = andalusia_group
	}
	allow = {
		is_at_war = no
		has_institution = bureaucracy
		has_institution = printing_press
		adm_tech = 19 #Res Publica
		num_of_provinces_owned_or_owned_by_non_sovereign_subjects_with = {
			province_group = andalusia_group
			value = 25 #10 + (0.5 * 29) = 24.5 -> 25
		}
		223 = { country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT }
		224 = { country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT }
		225 = { country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT }
		1748 = { country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT }
		10012 = { country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT }
	}
	effect = {
		#Integrate PUs, Domains, Fiefs
		every_subject_country = { 
			limit = { capital_scope = { province_group = andalusia_group } OR = { is_subject_of_type = personal_union is_subject_of_type = dominion is_subject_of_type = fief } }

# Iberia

			OR = { 
				government = native 
				government = tribal 
			} 
		}

			tag = LSA

			tag = SPI
			tag = VSC
			tag = ADL
			tag = ADU
			#tag = OCC
		}
	}
	provinces_to_highlight = {
		region = iberia_region
	}
	allow = {
		is_at_war = no

			region = iberia_region
			value = 160

			}

		adm_tech = 2 #Politics
		num_of_provinces_owned_or_owned_by_non_sovereign_subjects_with = {
			province_group = england_group
			value = 50 #
		}
		236 = { country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT }
		244 = { country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT }
		245 = { country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT }
		239 = { country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT }
	}
	effect = {
		#Integrate PUs, Domains, Fiefs
		every_subject_country = { 
			limit = { capital_scope = { province_group = england_group } OR = { is_subject_of_type = personal_union is_subject_of_type = dominion is_subject_of_type = fief } }
			custom_tooltip = IR_formable_integration
			hidden_effect = {
				overlord = {
					inherit = PREV
				}
			}
		}
		
		#Change Tag
		change_tag = ENG	
		
		#Set Govt Rank	
		if = { 
			limit = { NOT = { government_rank = 4 } }
			set_government_rank = 4
		}
		
		#Rewards
		add_prestige = 25
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = centralization_modifier
			duration = 7300
		}
		
		#Change Ideas
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_custom_ideas = no
				NOT = { has_idea_group = ENG_ideas }
			}
			country_event = { id = ideagroups.1 } #Swap Ideas
		}
		
		#Disable decision
		set_country_flag = formed_england_flag
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1
	}
	ai_importance = 400 #
}

# Ireland
AN_ireland_nation = { 
	major = yes
	potential = {
		NOT = { has_country_flag = formed_ireland_flag }
		IRE = { exists = no }
		NOT = { 
			OR = { 
				government = native 
				government = tribal 
				tag = ENG
				tag = GBR
				tag = UNK
				tag = WLS
				tag = SCO
				tag = ANI
				tag = WMC
			} 
		}
		primary_culture = irish
	}
	provinces_to_highlight = {
		region = ireland_area
	}
	allow = {
		is_at_war = no
		has_institution = bureaucracy
		adm_tech = 2 #Politics
		num_of_provinces_owned_or_owned_by_non_sovereign_subjects_with = {
			region = ireland_area
			value = 36 #22
		}
		373 = { country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT }
		3009 = { country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT }
		4118 = { country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT }
		375 = { country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT }
		376 = { country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT }
		4119 = { country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT }
		372 = { country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT }
		
	}
	effect = {
		#Integrate PUs, Domains, Fiefs
		every_subject_country = { 
			limit = { capital_scope = { region = ireland_area } OR = { is_subject_of_type = personal_union is_subject_of_type = dominion is_subject_of_type = fief } }
			custom_tooltip = IR_formable_integration
			hidden_effect = {
				overlord = {
					inherit = PREV
				}
			}
		}
		
		#Change Tag
		change_tag = IRE	
		
		#Set Govt Rank	
		if = { 
			limit = { NOT = { government_rank = 4 } }
			set_government_rank = 4
		}
		
		#Rewards
		add_prestige = 25
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = centralization_modifier
			duration = 7300
		}
		
		#Change Ideas
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_custom_ideas = no
				NOT = { has_idea_group = IRE_ideas }
			}
			country_event = { id = ideagroups.1 } #Swap Ideas
		}
		
		#Disable decision
		set_country_flag = formed_ireland_flag
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1
	}
	ai_importance = 400 #
}

		#Integrate PUs, Domains, Fiefs
		every_subject_country = { 
			limit = { capital_scope = { province_group = westphalia_group } OR = { is_subject_of_type = personal_union is_subject_of_type = dominion is_subject_of_type = fief } }
			custom_tooltip = IR_formable_integration
			hidden_effect = {
				overlord = {
					inherit = PREV
				}
			}
		}
		
		#Change Tag
		change_tag = WES
		
		#Set Govt Rank	
		if = { 
			limit = { NOT = { government_rank = 3 } }
			set_government_rank = 3
		}
		
		#Rewards
		add_prestige = 25
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = centralization_modifier
			duration = 7300
		}
		
		#Change Ideas
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_custom_ideas = no
				NOT = { has_idea_group = WES_ideas }
			}
			country_event = { id = ideagroups.1 } #Swap Ideas
		}
		
		#Disable decision
		set_country_flag = formed_westphalia_flag
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1
	}
	ai_importance = 400 #
}

				}

			limit = { capital_scope = { province_group = polabia_group } OR = { is_subject_of_type = personal_union is_subject_of_type = dominion is_subject_of_type = fief } }
			custom_tooltip = IR_formable_integration
			hidden_effect = {
				overlord = {
					inherit = PREV
				}
			}
		}
		
		#Change Tag
		change_tag = PLB
				
		#Set Govt Rank	
		if = { 
			limit = { NOT = { government_rank = 4 } }
			set_government_rank = 4
		}
		
		#Rewards
		add_prestige = 25
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = centralization_modifier
			duration = 7300
		}
		
		#Change Ideas
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_custom_ideas = no
				NOT = { has_idea_group = PLB_ideas }
			}
			country_event = { id = ideagroups.1 } #Swap Ideas
		}
		
		#Disable decision
		set_country_flag = formed_polabia_flag
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1
	}
	ai_importance = 400 #
}

		NOT = { has_country_flag = formed_piedmont_flag }
		PIE = { exists = no }
		NOT = { 
			OR = { 
				government = native 
				government = tribal 
				tag = SNS
				tag = LMB
				tag = EMR
				tag = RMG
				tag = TUS
				tag = LGA
				tag = UMB
				tag = PNP
				tag = TTS
				tag = DAL
				tag = ITA
				tag = PAP
			} 
		}
		primary_culture = piedmontese
	}
	provinces_to_highlight = {
		province_group = piedmont_group
	}
	allow = {
		is_at_war = no
		has_institution = bureaucracy
		has_institution = printing_press
		adm_tech = 19 #Res Publica
		num_of_provinces_owned_or_owned_by_non_sovereign_subjects_with = {
			province_group = piedmont_group
			value = 15 #? 10 (0.5 * 12) > 16 > 15
		}
		103 = { country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT }
		7058 = { country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT }
	}
	effect = {
		#Integrate PUs, Domains, Fiefs
		every_subject_country = { 
			limit = { capital_scope = { province_group = piedmont_group } OR = { is_subject_of_type = personal_union is_subject_of_type = dominion is_subject_of_type = fief } }
			custom_tooltip = IR_formable_integration
			hidden_effect = {
				overlord = {
					inherit = PREV
				}
			}
		}
		
		#Change Tag
		change_tag = PIE	
		
		#Set Govt Rank	
		if = { 
			limit = { NOT = { government_rank = 4 } }
			set_government_rank = 4
		}
		
		#Rewards
		add_prestige = 25
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = centralization_modifier
			duration = 7300
		}
		
		#Change Ideas
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_custom_ideas = no
				NOT = { has_idea_group = PIE_ideas }
			}
			country_event = { id = ideagroups.1 } #Swap Ideas
		}
		
		#Disable decision
		set_country_flag = formed_piedmont_flag
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1
	}
	ai_importance = 400 #
}

				}

		}

# Bosnia
AN_bosnia_nation = { 
	major = yes
	potential = {
		NOT = { has_country_flag = formed_bosnia_flag }
		BOS = { exists = no }
		NOT = { 
			OR = { 
				government = native 
				government = tribal 
				tag = HUN
				tag = ALB
				tag = SER
				tag = CRO
			} 
		}
		OR = {
			primary_culture = bosnian
			primary_culture = bosniak
		}
	}
	provinces_to_highlight = {
		province_group = bosnia_group
	}
	allow = {
		is_at_war = no
		has_institution = bureaucracy
		adm_tech = 2 #Politics
		num_of_provinces_owned_or_owned_by_non_sovereign_subjects_with = {
			province_group = bosnia_group
			value = 10 #14-4 = 10
		}
		140 = { country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT }
	}
	effect = {
		#Integrate PUs, Domains, Fiefs
		every_subject_country = { 
			limit = { capital_scope = { province_group = bosnia_group } OR = { is_subject_of_type = personal_union is_subject_of_type = dominion is_subject_of_type = fief } }
			custom_tooltip = IR_formable_integration
			hidden_effect = {
				overlord = {
					inherit = PREV
				}
			}
		}
		
		#Change Tag
		change_tag = BOS	
		
		#Set Govt Rank	
		if = { 
			limit = { NOT = { government_rank = 4 } }
			set_government_rank = 4
		}
		
		#Rewards
		add_prestige = 25
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = centralization_modifier
			duration = 7300
		}
		
		#Change Ideas
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_custom_ideas = no
				NOT = { has_idea_group = BOS_ideas }
			}
			country_event = { id = ideagroups.1 } #Swap Ideas
		}
		
		#Disable decision
		set_country_flag = formed_bosnia_flag
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1
	}
	ai_importance = 400 #
}

			OR = { 
				government = native 
				government = tribal

				tag = LIT

				tag = BTC
			} 
		}

			primary_culture = lithuanian

			primary_culture = samogitian
		}
	}
	provinces_to_highlight = {
		province_group = lithuania_group
	}
	allow = {
		is_at_war = no
		has_institution = bureaucracy
		adm_tech = 2 #Politics
		num_of_provinces_owned_or_owned_by_non_sovereign_subjects_with = {
			province_group = lithuania_group
			value = 20 #?
		}
		272 = { country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT }
	}
	effect = {
		#Integrate PUs, Domains, Fiefs
		every_subject_country = { 
			limit = { capital_scope = { province_group = lithuania_group } OR = { is_subject_of_type = personal_union is_subject_of_type = dominion is_subject_of_type = fief } }
			custom_tooltip = IR_formable_integration
			hidden_effect = {
				overlord = {
					inherit = PREV
				}
			}
		}
		
		#Change Tag
		change_tag = LIT	
		
		#Set Govt Rank	
		if = { 
			limit = { NOT = { government_rank = 4 } }
			set_government_rank = 4
		}
		
		#Rewards
		add_prestige = 25
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = centralization_modifier
			duration = 7300
		}
		
		#Change Ideas
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_custom_ideas = no
				NOT = { has_idea_group = LIT_ideas }
			}
			country_event = { id = ideagroups.1 } #Swap Ideas
		}
		
		#Disable decision
		set_country_flag = formed_lithuania_flag
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1
	}
	ai_importance = 400 #
}

		num_of_provinces_owned_or_owned_by_non_sovereign_subjects_with = {
			province_group = crimea_group
			value = 10 #14 total
		}
		2410 = { country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT }
		285 = { country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT }
	}
	effect = {
		#Integrate PUs, Domains, Fiefs
		every_subject_country = {
			limit = { capital_scope = { province_group = crimea_group } OR = { is_subject_of_type = personal_union is_subject_of_type = dominion is_subject_of_type = fief } }
			custom_tooltip = IR_formable_integration
			hidden_effect = {
				overlord = {
					inherit = PREV
				}
			}
		}
		
		#Change Tag
		change_tag = TR1	
		
		#Set Govt Rank	
		if = { 
			limit = { NOT = { government_rank = 3 } }
			set_government_rank = 3
		}
		
		#Rewards
		add_prestige = 25
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = centralization_modifier
			duration = 7300
		}
		
		#Name
		if = {
			limit = { culture_group = armenian_group }
			overide_country_name = TAURICIA
			change_primary_culture = ghrimahayer	
		}
		
		#Change Ideas
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_custom_ideas = no
				NOT = { has_idea_group = TR1_ideas }
			}
			country_event = { id = ideagroups.1 } #Swap Ideas
		}
		
		#Disable decision
		set_country_flag = formed_tauricia_flag
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1
	}
	ai_importance = 400 #
}

# Crete
AN_crete_nation = {
	major = yes
	potential = {
		NOT = { has_country_flag = formed_crete_flag }
		CRT = { exists = no }
		GRE = { exists = no }
		NOT = {
			OR = {
				government = native
				government = tribal
				tag = BYZ
				tag = MCD
				tag = THS
				tag = HL5
				tag = EPI
				tag = A3G
				tag = PEL
				tag = THR
				tag = GRE
			}
		}
		culture_group = byzantine_g
		capital_scope = { area = eastern_mediterrenean_islands_area }
	}
	provinces_to_highlight = {
		area = eastern_mediterrenean_islands_area
	}
	allow = {
		is_at_war = no
		has_institution = bureaucracy
		adm_tech = 2 #Politics
		num_of_provinces_owned_or_owned_by_non_sovereign_subjects_with = {
			area = eastern_mediterrenean_islands_area
			value = 3 #?
		}
		163 = { country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT }
	}
	effect = {
		#Integrate PUs, Domains, Fiefs
		every_subject_country = { 
			limit = { capital_scope = { area = eastern_mediterrenean_islands_area } OR = { is_subject_of_type = personal_union is_subject_of_type = dominion is_subject_of_type = fief } }
			custom_tooltip = IR_formable_integration
			hidden_effect = {
				overlord = {
					inherit = PREV
				}
			}
		}
		
		#Change Tag
		change_tag = CRT	
		
		#Set Govt Rank	
		if = { 
			limit = { NOT = { government_rank = 4 } }
			set_government_rank = 4
		}
		
		#Rewards
		add_prestige = 25
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = centralization_modifier
			duration = 7300
		}
		
		#Change Ideas
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_custom_ideas = no
				NOT = { has_idea_group = CRT_ideas }
			}
			country_event = { id = ideagroups.1 } #Swap Ideas
		}
		
		#Disable decision
		set_country_flag = formed_crete_flag
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1
	}
	ai_importance = 400 #
}

# Phoenicia
AN_phoenicia_nation = {
	major = yes
	potential = {
		NOT = { has_country_flag = formed_phoenicia_flag }
		PHO = { exists = no }
		NOT = {
			OR = {
				government = native
				government = tribal
				tag = BYZ
				tag = TUR
				tag = RUM
				tag = MAM
				tag = PER
				tag = TIM
				tag = MUG
			}
		}
		primary_culture = maronite
	}
	provinces_to_highlight = {
		province_group = phoenicia_group
	}
	allow = {
		is_at_war = no
		has_institution = bureaucracy
		adm_tech = 2 #Politics
		num_of_provinces_owned_or_owned_by_non_sovereign_subjects_with = {
			province_group = phoenicia_group
			value = 15 #8 + (0.5 * 14) = 15
		}
		10935 = { country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT }
		10236 = { country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT }
	}
	effect = {
		#Integrate PUs, Domains, Fiefs
		every_subject_country = {
			limit = { capital_scope = {	province_group = phoenicia_group } OR = { is_subject_of_type = personal_union is_subject_of_type = dominion is_subject_of_type = fief } }
			custom_tooltip = IR_formable_integration
			hidden_effect = {
				overlord = {
					inherit = PREV
				}
			}
		}

		#Change Tag
		change_tag = PHO

		#Set Govt Rank
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { government_rank = 4 } }
			set_government_rank = 4
		}

		#Rewards
		add_prestige = 25
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = centralization_modifier
			duration = 7300
		}

		#Change Ideas
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_custom_ideas = no
				NOT = { has_idea_group = PHO_ideas }
			}
			country_event = { id = ideagroups.1 } #Swap Ideas
		}

		#Disable decision
		set_country_flag = formed_phoenicia_flag
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1
	}
	ai_importance = 400 #
}

# Oman
AN_oman_nation = {
	major = yes
	potential = {
		NOT = { has_country_flag = formed_oman_flag }
		OMA = { exists = no }
		NOT = {
			OR = {
				government = native
				government = tribal
				tag = BYZ
				tag = TUR
				tag = RUM
				tag = MAM
				tag = PER
				tag = TIM
				tag = MUG
				tag = BHR
				tag = QTR
				tag = ALH
				tag = YEM
				tag = HDR
				tag = NJR
				tag = ARB
			}
		}
		culture_group = omani_culture
	}
	provinces_to_highlight = {
		province_group = oman_group
	}
	allow = {
		is_at_war = no
		has_institution = bureaucracy
		adm_tech = 2 #Politics
		num_of_provinces_owned_or_owned_by_non_sovereign_subjects_with = {
			province_group = oman_group
			value = 15 #7 + (0.5 * 26) -5 = 15
		}
		400 = { country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT }
	}
	effect = {
		#Integrate PUs, Domains, Fiefs
		every_subject_country = {
			limit = { capital_scope = { province_group = oman_group } OR = { is_subject_of_type = personal_union is_subject_of_type = dominion is_subject_of_type = fief } }
			custom_tooltip = IR_formable_integration
			hidden_effect = {
				overlord = {
					inherit = PREV
				}
			}
		}

		#Change Tag
		change_tag = OMA

		#Set Govt Rank
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { government_rank = 4 } }
			set_government_rank = 4
		}
		
		#Rewards
		add_prestige = 25
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = centralization_modifier
			duration = 7300
		}
		
		#Change Ideas
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_custom_ideas = no
				NOT = { has_idea_group = OMA_ideas }
			}
			country_event = { id = ideagroups.1 } #Swap Ideas
		}
		
		#Disable decision
		set_country_flag = formed_oman_flag
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1
	}
	ai_importance = 400 #
}

		5264 = { country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT }
		358 = { country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT }
	}
	effect = {
		#Integrate PUs, Domains, Fiefs
		every_subject_country = { 
			limit = { capital_scope = { region = egypt_region } OR = { is_subject_of_type = personal_union is_subject_of_type = dominion is_subject_of_type = fief } }
			custom_tooltip = IR_formable_integration
			hidden_effect = {
				overlord = {
					inherit = PREV
				}
			}
		}
		
		#Change Tag
		change_tag = EGY	
		
		#Set Govt Rank	
		if = { 
			limit = { NOT = { government_rank = 4 } }
			set_government_rank = 4
		}
		
		#Rewards
		add_prestige = 25
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = centralization_modifier
			duration = 7300
		}
		
		#Change Ideas
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_custom_ideas = no
				NOT = { has_idea_group = EGY_ideas }
			}
			country_event = { id = ideagroups.1 } #Swap Ideas
		}
		
		#Disable decision
		set_country_flag = formed_egypt_flag
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1
	}
	ai_importance = 400 #
}

	provinces_to_highlight = {
		region = deccan_region
	}
	allow = {
		is_at_war = no
		has_institution = bureaucracy
		has_institution = printing_press
		adm_tech = 19 #Res Publica
		num_of_provinces_owned_or_owned_by_non_sovereign_subjects_with = {
			region = deccan_region
			value = 100 #?
		}
		capital_scope = { region = deccan_region }
		4421 = { country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT }
		541 = { country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT }
		1948 = { country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT }
		545 = { country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT }
		569 = { country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT }
		4432 = { country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT }
	}
	effect = {
		#Integrate PUs, Domains, Fiefs
		every_subject_country = {
			limit = { capital_scope = { region = deccan_region } OR = { is_subject_of_type = personal_union is_subject_of_type = dominion is_subject_of_type = fief } }
			custom_tooltip = IR_formable_integration
			hidden_effect = {
				overlord = {
					inherit = PREV
				}
			}
		}
		
		#Change Tag
		change_tag = DEC	
		
		#Set Govt Rank	
		if = { 
			limit = { NOT = { government_rank = 5 } }
			set_government_rank = 5
		}
		
		#Rewards
		add_prestige = 25
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = centralization_modifier
			duration = 7300
		}
		
		#Change Ideas
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_custom_ideas = no
				NOT = { has_idea_group = DEC_ideas }
			}
			country_event = { id = ideagroups.1 } #Swap Ideas
		}
		
		#Disable decision
		set_country_flag = formed_deccan_flag
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1
	}
	ai_importance = 400 #
}

		num_of_provinces_owned_or_owned_by_non_sovereign_subjects_with = {
			region = borneo_region
			value = 40 #?
		}
		639 = { country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT }
		2709 = { country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT }
		11395 = { country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT }
		6461 = { country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT }
		2705 = { country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT }
		capital_scope = { region = borneo_region }
	}
	effect = {
		#Integrate PUs, Domains, Fiefs
		every_subject_country = {
			limit = { capital_scope = { region = borneo_region } OR = { is_subject_of_type = personal_union is_subject_of_type = dominion is_subject_of_type = fief } }
			custom_tooltip = IR_formable_integration
			hidden_effect = {
				overlord = {
					inherit = PREV
				}
			}
		}

		#Change Tag
		change_tag = BOR

		#Set Govt Rank
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { government_rank = 4 } }
			set_government_rank = 4
		}

		#Rewards
		add_prestige = 25
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = centralization_modifier
			duration = 7300
		}
		
		#Change Ideas
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_custom_ideas = no
				NOT = { has_idea_group = BOR_ideas }
			}
			country_event = { id = ideagroups.1 } #Swap Ideas
		}
		
		#Disable decision
		set_country_flag = formed_borneo_flag
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1
	}
	ai_importance = 400 #
}

		adm_tech = 2 #Politics

		#Integrate PUs, Domains, Fiefs

			limit = { capital_scope = { province_group = sokoto_group } OR = { is_subject_of_type = personal_union is_subject_of_type = dominion is_subject_of_type = fief } }
			custom_tooltip = IR_formable_integration

					inherit = PREV
				}
			}
		}

			}
			country_event = { id = ideagroups.1 } #Swap Ideas
		}

		#Disable decision
		set_country_flag = formed_sokoto_flag
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1
	}
	ai_importance = 400 #
}

		add_country_modifier = {
			name = centralization_modifier
			duration = 7300
		}

		#Change Ideas
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_custom_ideas = no
				NOT = { has_idea_group = QUE_ideas }
			}
			country_event = { id = ideagroups.1 } #Swap Ideas
		}

		#Disable decision
		set_country_flag = formed_quebec_flag
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1
	}
	ai_importance = 400 #
}

#United States/America
AN_united_states_nation = {
	major = yes
	potential = {
		NOT = { has_country_flag = formed_united_states_flag }
		USA = { exists = no }
		NOT = {
			OR = {
				government = native
				government = tribal
			}
			tag = CAN
			tag = QUE
			tag = FLO
			tag = ORL
			tag = TEX
			tag = CAL
			tag = CSC
			tag = ALA
		}
		is_former_colonial_nation = yes
		capital_scope = { province_group = united_states_group }
	}
	provinces_to_highlight = {
		province_group = united_states_group
	}
	allow = {
		is_at_war = no
		has_institution = bureaucracy
		has_institution = printing_press
		has_institution = state_sovereignty
		adm_tech = 30 #Absolutism
		num_of_provinces_owned_or_owned_by_non_sovereign_subjects_with = {
			province_group = united_states_group
			value = 120 #134-14 = 120
		}
	}
	effect = {
		#Integrate PUs, Domains, Fiefs
		every_subject_country = {
			limit = { capital_scope = { province_group = united_states_group } OR = { is_subject_of_type = personal_union is_subject_of_type = dominion is_subject_of_type = fief } }
			custom_tooltip = IR_formable_integration
			hidden_effect = {
				overlord = {
					inherit = PREV
				}
			}
		}

		#Change Tag
		change_tag = USA

		#Set Govt Rank
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { government_rank = 4 } }
			set_government_rank = 4
		}

		#Rewards
		add_prestige = 25
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = centralization_modifier
			duration = 7300
		}

		#Change Ideas
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_custom_ideas = no
				NOT = { has_idea_group = USA_ideas }
			}
			country_event = { id = ideagroups.1 } #Swap Ideas
		}

		#Disable decision
		set_country_flag = formed_united_states_flag
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1
	}
	ai_importance = 400 #
}

			tag = CAL
			tag = CSC

	}
	provinces_to_highlight = {
		colonial_region = colonial_florida
	}
	allow = {
		is_at_war = no
		has_institution = bureaucracy
		has_institution = printing_press
		has_institution = state_sovereignty
		adm_tech = 30 #Absolutism
		num_of_provinces_owned_or_owned_by_non_sovereign_subjects_with = {
			colonial_region = colonial_florida
			value = 20 #33- 13 = 20
		}
	}
	effect = {
		#Integrate PUs, Domains, Fiefs
		every_subject_country = {
			limit = { capital_scope = { colonial_region = colonial_florida } OR = { is_subject_of_type = personal_union is_subject_of_type = dominion is_subject_of_type = fief } }
			custom_tooltip = IR_formable_integration
			hidden_effect = {
				overlord = {
					inherit = PREV
				}
			}
		}

		#Change Tag
		change_tag = FLO

		#Set Govt Rank
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { government_rank = 4 } }
			set_government_rank = 4
		}

		#Rewards
		add_prestige = 25
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = centralization_modifier

		}

			limit = {
				has_custom_ideas = no
				NOT = { has_idea_group = FLO_ideas }
			}

		}

	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1
	}
	ai_importance = 400 #

			value = 30 #?
		}
	}
	effect = {
		#Integrate PUs, Domains, Fiefs
		every_subject_country = {
			limit = { capital_scope = { region = colombia_region } OR = { is_subject_of_type = personal_union is_subject_of_type = dominion is_subject_of_type = fief } }
			custom_tooltip = IR_formable_integration
			hidden_effect = {
				overlord = {
					inherit = PREV
				}
			}
		}

		#Change Tag
		change_tag = COL

		#Set Govt Rank
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { government_rank = 4 } }
			set_government_rank = 4
		}

		#Rewards
		add_prestige = 25
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = centralization_modifier
			duration = 7300
		}

		#Change Ideas
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_custom_ideas = no
				NOT = { has_idea_group = COL_ideas }
			}
			country_event = { id = ideagroups.1 } #Swap Ideas
		}

		#Disable decision
		set_country_flag = formed_colombia_flag
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1
	}
	ai_importance = 400 #
}

# Qing China
AN_qing_nation = {
	major = yes
	potential = {
		NOT = { has_country_flag = formed_qing_flag }
		QNG = { exists = no }
		culture_group = evenks
	}
	provinces_to_highlight = {
		province_group = greater_china_group
	}
	allow = {
		is_at_war = no
		has_institution = bureaucracy
		adm_tech = 2 #Politics
		num_of_provinces_owned_or_owned_by_non_sovereign_subjects_with = {
			province_group = greater_china_group
			value = 200 #because why not
		}
		1816 = { country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT }
		726 = { country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT }
		730 = { country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT }
		700 = { country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT }
		1821 = { country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT }
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_dlc = "Mandate of Heaven"
				any_country = {
					is_emperor_of_china = yes
				}
			}
			is_emperor_of_china = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_dlc = "Common Sense"
			}
			government_rank = 5
		}
		else = {
			total_development = 1000
		}
	}
	effect = {
		#Integrate PUs, Domains, Fiefs
		every_subject_country = {
			limit = { capital_scope = { province_group = greater_china_group } OR = { is_subject_of_type = personal_union is_subject_of_type = dominion is_subject_of_type = fief } }
			custom_tooltip = IR_formable_integration
			hidden_effect = {
				overlord = {
					inherit = PREV
				}
			}
		}

		#Change Tag
		change_tag = QNG

		#Set Govt Rank
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { government_rank = 5 } }
			set_government_rank = 5
		}

		#Rewards
		add_prestige = 25
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = centralization_modifier
			duration = 7300
		}

		#Change Ideas
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_custom_ideas = no
				NOT = { has_idea_group = QNG_ideas }
			}
			country_event = { id = ideagroups.1 } #Swap Ideas
		}

		#Disable decision
		set_country_flag = formed_qing_flag
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1
	}
	ai_importance = 400 #
}
